              <h2 class="heading">St. Regis Connoisseur</h2>
                    <div class="wide copy"><p>Meet our global tastemaker who embodies the modern glamour of St. Regis.</p>

      	  <div class="reversed-headings">
	      	        <h2 class="divider heading">Nacho Figueras</h2>
	      	      	  </div>
                    <div class="copy"><p><span class="s1">Nacho Figueras is the most recognized polo player in the world. Known for his sportsmanship, skill and impeccable sense of style, both on and off the field, Nacho Figueras serves as the first-ever Connoisseur for St. Regis.</span></p>

    <div class="info">
              <h2 class="heading">A Legacy in Time</h2>
                      </div>
  </div>

	<div class="foreground">

								<img srcset="https://st-regis.marriott.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/78202_m_sq-400x400.jpg, https://st-regis.marriott.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/78202_m_sq-768x768.jpg 2x" alt="Caroline Astor in Evening Dress Putting on Corsage">
							</picture>
													</div>
						<div class="tab-content-panel">
							<div class="reversed-headings">
																	<h2 class="heading">The Caroline Astor</h2>
																							</div>
															<div class="copy"><p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Many of our most cherished rituals are inspired by the tirelessly inventive mind of Gilded Age doyenne, Caroline Astor. She invited only a select</span><span style="font-weight: 400;"> 400 acquaintances, friends and luminaries to private teas, midnight suppers and affluent galas</span><span style="font-weight: 400;">, creating</span><span style="font-weight: 400;"> Americas first high society register. As artists, visionaries and influencers of all kinds vied for inclusion, her social circle evolved to shape the first true expression of New York society.</span></p>
</div>
																				</div>
					</div>
				</div>
							<div class="tab-content-panels-container-mobile">
					<div class="tab-label-mobile" data-tab-index="7">1904<span class="icon-carret"></span></div>
					<div class="wrapper slides-target">
												<div class="image-mobile">
							<picture>
								<source srcset="https://st-regis.marriott.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/76134_wide-1536x864.jpg, https://st-regis.marriott.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/76134_wide.jpg 2x" media="(min-width: 1137px)">
								<source srcset="https://st-regis.marriott.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/76134_wide-1136x639.jpg, https://st-regis.marriott.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/76134_wide-2560x1440.jpg 2x" media="(min-width: 769px)">
								<source srcset="https://st-regis.marriott.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/76134_m_sq-768x768.jpg, https://st-regis.marriott.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/76134_m_sq-1536x1536.jpg 2x" media="(min-width: 401px)">
								<img srcset="https://st-regis.marriott.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/76134_m_sq-400x400.jpg, https://st-regis.marriott.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/76134_m_sq-768x768.jpg 2x" alt="Portrait Of Financier John Jacob Astor">
							</picture>
													</div>
						<div class="tab-content-panel">
							<div class="reversed-headings">
																	<h2 class="heading">An Extraordinary Life</h2>
																							</div>
															<div class="copy"><p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Caroline Astor&#8217;s son, Colonel John Jacob Astor IV, introduced The St. Regis New York in 1904 to immediate acclaim, with </span><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">The New York Times</span></i><span style="font-weight: 400;"> declaring it &#8220;the finest hotel in America.&#8221; A true visionary, inventor and entrepreneur John Jacob Astor ensured the original St. Regis was as technologically advanced as it was luxurious, insisting that each room have its own telephone. Astor </span><span style="font-weight: 400;">perished during the sinking of the Titanic on April 15, 1912. </span><span style="font-weight: 400;">More than a century later, the legacy of one of the Titanics wealthiest and most famous passengers lives on through the continued growth and evolution of St. Regis. </span></p>
</div>
																				</div>
					</div>
				</div>
							<div class="tab-content-panels-container-mobile">
					<div class="tab-label-mobile" data-tab-index="7">1932<span class="icon-carret"></span></div>
					<div class="wrapper slides-target">
												<div class="captioned image-mobile">
							<picture>
								<source srcset="https://st-regis.marriott.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/148322_wide-1536x864.jpg, https://st-regis.marriott.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/148322_wide.jpg 2x" media="(min-width: 1137px)">
								<source srcset="https://st-regis.marriott.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/148322_wide-1136x639.jpg, https://st-regis.marriott.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/148322_wide-2560x1440.jpg 2x" media="(min-width: 769px)">
								<source srcset="https://st-regis.marriott.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/148322_m_sq-768x768.jpg, https://st-regis.marriott.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/148322_m_sq-1536x1536.jpg 2x" media="(min-width: 401px)">
								<img srcset="https://st-regis.marriott.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/148322_m_sq-400x400.jpg, https://st-regis.marriott.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/148322_m_sq-768x768.jpg 2x" alt="Old King Cole mural at St. Regis New York">
							</picture>
															<div class="caption">St. Regis New York - King Cole Bar and Restaurant</div>
													</div>
						<div class="tab-content-panel">
							<div class="reversed-headings">
																	<h2 class="heading">A Captivating Addition</h2>
																							</div>
															<div class="copy"><p><span class="s1">The Old King Cole mural, an original work by celebrated artist Maxfield Parrish, is unveiled at The St. Regis New York. This iconic work of art has become the inspiration for other mural paintings to be displayed throughout most of our St. Regis Hotels &amp; Resorts.</span></p>
</div>
																				</div>
					</div>
				</div>
							<div class="tab-content-panels-container-mobile">

								<source srcset="https://st-regis.marriott.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/130821_wide-1136x639.jpg, https://st-regis.marriott.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/130821_wide-2560x1440.jpg 2x" media="(min-width: 769px)">

								<img srcset="https://st-regis.marriott.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/130821_m_sq-400x400.jpg, https://st-regis.marriott.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/130821_m_sq-768x768.jpg 2x" alt="Original Bloody Mary illustration">
							</picture>

						<div class="tab-content-panel">
							<div class="reversed-headings">
																	<h2 class="heading">The Original Bloody Mary</h2>
																							</div>
															<div class="copy"><p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The St. Regis New York head bartender, Fernand Petiot, creates the iconic Bloody Mary cocktail which lead to unique Bloody Mary creations for St. Regis around the world.</span></p>
</div>
																				</div>
					</div>

							</picture>
													</div>
						<div class="tab-content-panel">
							<div class="reversed-headings">
																	<h2 class="heading">An Evolving Legacy</h2>
																							</div>
															<div class="copy"><p><span style="font-weight: 400;">St. Regis redefined the luxury hotel in 1904, and more than 100 years later this quintessential lifestyle has expanded to more than 40 St. Regis hotels and resorts around the world. </span></p>
</div>
																				</div>
					</div>
				</div>
							<div class="tab-content-panels-container-mobile">
					<div class="tab-label-mobile" data-tab-index="7">2010<span class="icon-carret"></span></div>
					<div class="wrapper slides-target">
												<div class="image-mobile">

								<source srcset="https://st-regis.marriott.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/208355_wide-1136x639.jpg, https://st-regis.marriott.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/208355_wide-2560x1440.jpg 2x" media="(min-width: 769px)">

							<div class="reversed-headings">
																	<h2 class="heading">St. Regis Connoisseurs</h2>
																							</div>
															<div class="copy"><p><span style="font-weight: 400;">St. Regis began its Connoisseur program in 2010 with the renowned Argentinian polo star, Nacho Figueras. Today, we are honored to include notable luxury fashion designers, exceptional musical talents and other outstanding tastemakers in this program who share our innovative spirit and tradition of excellence.</span></p>
</div>
																				</div>
					</div>
				</div>

																	<h2 class="heading">Live Exquisite</h2>
																							</div>
															<div class="copy"><p><span style="font-weight: 400;">For St. Regis, to Live Exquisite is about creating unforgettable experiences for our guests, especially families. Therefore, our Family Traditions program was crafted to celebrate togetherness by experiencing a destination in its truest form.</span></p>
</div>
																				</div>

</div>  <div class="curator-load-more-button-wrapper">

      View More    </button>
  </div>

  <script>
    var visiblePosts = parseInt('10');
    var maxPosts = parseInt('88');
    var buttons = document.getElementsByClassName("curator-load-more-button");
    var totalPosts = 10;
    
    for (let index = 0; index < buttons.length; index++) {
      const button = buttons[index];
      button.onclick = function(e) {showNextRow(e)};
    }

    function showNextRow(e) {
      visiblePosts = visiblePosts + parseInt(e.currentTarget.getAttribute('data-load'));
      
      // hide the button if all posts are loaded
      if(visiblePosts >= maxPosts) {
        e.currentTarget.style.display = 'none';
      }

      // collect all the cards
      var cards = Array.from(e.currentTarget.parentElement.previousElementSibling.children);

      // toggle card classes
      updateVisiblePosts(visiblePosts, cards)
      
    }

    function updateVisiblePosts(visiblePosts, cards) {
      cards.forEach(function (card, idx) {
        if(idx < visiblePosts) {
          card.classList.remove('curator-card-hidden')
        }
      });
    }
  </script>

The use of Empire Rye,* distilled only in New York at some of the State\u2019s oldest distilleries, introduces a tantalizing flavor profile and sense of place of <a href=\"https:\/\/www.srresidencesrye.com\/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">The St. Regis Residences, Rye<\/a>. Add Empire Rye. Fill glass with mix, stir vigorously and garnish with filet mignon bite and Scotch Quail Egg.<\/p>\n<p><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">Empire Bloody Mary Mix<br \/>\n<\/span><i>Spice Mix:<br \/>\n<\/i>1 tsp\/ 4 g salt<br \/>\n1 tsp\/ 4 g of Fresh-ground black peppercorn<br \/>\n1 tsp\/ 4 g Dried Basil*<i>*<br \/>\n<\/i>1 tsp\/ 4 g Dried Oregano*<i>*<br \/>\n<\/i>1 tsp\/ 4 g Dried Rosemary*<i>*<br \/>\n<\/i>1 tsp\/ 4 g Dried Thyme*<i>*<br \/>\n<\/i>1 pinch Cayenne Pepper<\/p>\n<p>3 cups\/ 720 ml organic, locally grown tomato juice<br \/>\n2 tsp\/ 10 ml Horseradish, or to taste<br \/>\n3 dashes Worcestershire Sauce<br \/>\n1 oz\/ 30 ml pickle juice or to taste<br \/>\n2 tbsp\/ 24 g Spice Mix\u00a0<i>(see above)<\/i><\/p>\n<p>Mix all spices together and set aside. Combine all liquid ingredients and add in 2 tbsp\/ 24 g of spice mix. Use immediately. Yields about 3 cups \/ 720 ml.<\/p>\n<p><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><i>Scotch Quail Egg<br \/>\n<\/i><\/span>12 quail eggs<br \/>\n1 lb\/ 400g Ground Beef or Sausage<br \/>\n2 sprigs of fresh thyme<br \/>\n1 large egg<br \/>\n1 cup\/ 100 g breadcrumbs<br \/>\nFlour<br \/>\nPinch of sea salt<br \/>\nPinch of white pepper<br \/>\nOil, for frying<\/p>\n<p>Boil quail eggs for 2 minutes. Strain eggs and place in cold water. Once cold, carefully peel eggs. While the eggs chill, mix the meat, thyme, salt and pepper. Divide mixture into 12 equal parts and use it to wrap peeled quail eggs. Dredge the wrapped eggs in flour. Whisk the hen\u2019s egg and coat the quail eggs in whisked egg and then in breadcrumbs.
